             const emptyState = document.getElementById(\'emptyState\');\n                \n                let filteredCodes = this.getFilteredCodes();\n                \n                if            \n                container.style.display = \'block\';\n                emptyState.style.display = \'none\';\n                \n                container.innerHTML = filteredCodes.map(code                         <div class="code-number">${code.code}</div>\n                            <div class="code-status status-${code.status}">${code.status.toUpperCase()}</div>\n <span class="category-badge category-${code.category}">${code.category}</span>\n                            <span style="color: #666; font-size: 14px;">Created ${createdDate} ‚Ä¢ ${daysActive} days * 60 * 24));\n                const baseProgress = Math.min(daysActive * 2, 50); // 2% per day, max 50%\n                const syncBonus = Math.min((code.synchronicities?.length || 0) * 10, 30); //    content: selectedMessage,\n                    type: messageType,\n                    category: category,\n                    stage: journeyStage,\n                    context:    const startDate = new Date(this.userSession.startTime);\n        const now = new Date();\n        const daysActive = Math.floor((now - startDate) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));\n        \n        if           document.getElementById(\'journeyProgress\').textContent = progressPercent + \'%\';\n                document.getElementById(\'stepCount\').textContent = stepCount;\n                \n                // Update progress ring\n                const progressCircle = document.querySelector(\'.progress-ring .progress\');\n                const circumference = 2 * Math.PI * 54;\n                const offset = circumference - (progressPercent / 100) * circumference;\n                progressCircle.style.strokeDashoffset = offset;\n                \n                // Update active codes\n \n                // Load recent codes\n                this.loadRecentCodes();\n                \n                // Update community stats\n                const echoCount =         }\n\n            loadRecentActivity() {\n                const container = document.getElementById(\'recentActivity\');\n                const activities = [];\n                \n
